assignment questions

import sqlite3

conn = sqlite3.connect("bigfive.db")
cursor = conn.cursor()

# Starter schema - you must add the remaining columns
# The pattern is: E1-E10, N1-N10, A1-A10, C1-C10, O1-O10
# All are INTEGER type (responses 1-5)
cursor.execute("DROP TABLE IF EXISTS responses")

cursor.execute("""
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS responses (
        id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        race INTEGER,
        age INTEGER,
        engnat INTEGER,
        gender INTEGER,
        hand INTEGER,
        source INTEGER,
        country TEXT,
        E1 INTEGER,
        E2 INTEGER,
        E3 INTEGER,
        E4 INTEGER,
        E5 INTEGER,
        E6 INTEGER,
        E7 INTEGER,
        E8 INTEGER,
        E9 INTEGER,
        E10 INTEGER,
        N1 INTEGER,
        N2 INTEGER,
        N3 INTEGER,
        N4 INTEGER,
        N5 INTEGER,
        N6 INTEGER,
        N7 INTEGER,
        N8 INTEGER,
        N9 INTEGER,
        N10 INTEGER,
        A1 INTEGER,
        A2 INTEGER,
        A3 INTEGER,
        A4 INTEGER,
        A5 INTEGER,
        A6 INTEGER,
        A7 INTEGER,
        A8 INTEGER,
        A9 INTEGER,
        A10 INTEGER,
        C1 INTEGER,
        C2 INTEGER,
        C3 INTEGER,
        C4 INTEGER,
        C5 INTEGER,
        C6 INTEGER,
        C7 INTEGER,
        C8 INTEGER,
        C9 INTEGER ,
        C10 INTEGER,
        O1 INTEGER,
        O2 INTEGER,
        O3 INTEGER,
        O4 INTEGER,
        O5 INTEGER,
        O6 INTEGER,
        O7 INTEGER,
        O8 INTEGER,
        O9 INTEGER,
        O10 INTEGER
    )
""")

conn.commit()
import csv

data = []

with open("data.csv", "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
    reader = csv.DictReader(f, delimiter = "\t")
    for row in reader:
        data.append((
            row['race'], row['age'], row['engnat'], row['gender'], row['hand'], row['source'], row['country'], row['E1'], row['E2'], row['E3'], row['E4'], row['E5'], row['E6'], row['E7'], row['E8'], row['E9'], row['E10'], row['N1'], row['N2'], row['N3'], row['N4'], row['N5'], row['N6'], row['N7'], row['N8'], row['N9'], row['N10'], row['A1'], row['A2'], row['A3'], row['A4'], row['A5'], row['A6'], row['A7'], row['A8'], row['A9'], row['A10'], row['C1'], row['C2'], row['C3'], row['C4'], row['C5'], row['C6'], row['C7'], row['C8'], row['C9'], row['C10'], row['O1'], row['O2'], row['O3'], row['O4'], row['O5'], row['O6'], row['O7'], row['O8'], row['O9'], row['O10']
        ))
cursor.executemany("""
    INSERT INTO responses (
        race, age, engnat, gender, hand, source, country,
        E1, E2, E3, E4, E5, E6, E7, E8, E9, E10,
        N1, N2, N3, N4, N5, N6, N7, N8, N9, N10,
        A1, A2, A3, A4, A5, A6, A7, A8, A9, A10,
        C1, C2, C3, C4, C5, C6, C7, C8, C9, C10,
        O1, O2, O3, O4, O5, O6, O7, O8, O9, O10
    )
    VALUES (
        ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?,
        ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?,
        ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?,
        ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?,
        ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?,
        ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?
    )
""", data)

conn.commit()
cursor.execute("SELECT * FROM responses LIMIT 5;")
rows = cursor.fetchall()

for r in rows:
    print(r)

# question 1: how many participants are there? 

cursor.execute("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM responses;")
print(cursor.fetchone()[0])
19719
# question 2: what is the mean age?

cursor.execute("""
SELECT ROUND(AVG(age), 2)
FROM responses
WHERE age BETWEEN 10 AND 100;
""")

print(cursor.fetchone()[0])
26.26
# question 3: mean score on E1 by gender 

cursor.execute("""
SELECT gender, ROUND(AVG(E1), 2)
FROM responses
GROUP BY gender;
""")

for row in cursor.fetchall():
    print(row)
(0, 2.46)
(1, 2.62)
(2, 2.64)
(3, 2.15)
# question 4: computing a total extraversion score for each participant (E1 to E10)

cursor.execute("""
SELECT id,
       (E1+E2+E3+E4+E5+E6+E7+E8+E9+E10) AS Extraversion
FROM responses
""")

for row in cursor.fetchall():
    print(row)

(19718, 29)
(19719, 28)
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import numpy as np

# Fetch age and total Extraversion score from the database
cursor.execute("""
SELECT age,
       (E1 + E2 + E3 + E4 + E5 + E6 + E7 + E8 + E9 + E10) AS extraversion_score
FROM responses
WHERE age BETWEEN 10 AND 100;
""")
data = cursor.fetchall()

# Convert to numpy arrays for convenience
data_array = np.array(data)
ages = data_array[:, 0]
extraversion_scores = data_array[:, 1]

# Optional: scale marker sizes based on score magnitude
marker_size = (extraversion_scores / np.max(extraversion_scores) * 50) + 10

# Create figure and axes
fig, ax = plt.subplots()

# Scatter plot
scatter = ax.scatter(ages, extraversion_scores, s=marker_size, c=extraversion_scores, 
                     cmap='viridis', alpha=0.7, edgecolor='k')

# Labels and title
ax.set_xlabel("Age", fontsize=12)
ax.set_ylabel("Extraversion Score", fontsize=12)
ax.set_title("Age vs Extraversion Score", fontsize=14)

# Optional: add colorbar to show score intensity
cbar = fig.colorbar(scatter, ax=ax)
cbar.set_label('Extraversion Score', fontsize=12)

ax.grid(True)
fig.tight_layout()

plt.show()
